| 80 | - **Role/domain:** Workflow; audit. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 81 | - **Caution:** A visually attractive chart still fails if numerical, labeling, or rendering checks fail. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 82 | - **Identifiers:** AV-100; TR visualization and geometry sections. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 83 | ### Stage 1: establish the reference | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 84 | - **Definition:** The audit step in which the Fv convention, canonical sequence, ratio definitions, limits, and relevant TR/REF values are fixed before inspecting a representation. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 85 | - **Role/domain:** Workflow. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 86 | - **Caution:** Skipping this stage invites convention mixing and index drift. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 87 | - **Identifiers:** TR-001--TR-015; REF-001--REF-030; AV-001, AV-004. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 88 | ### Stage 2: inspect a representation | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 89 | - **Definition:** The audit step in which the chart, diagram, image, table, or prose is examined for visible data, labels, scales, geometry, and rendering features. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 90 | - **Role/domain:** Workflow; image audit. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 91 | - **Caution:** Separate visible evidence from calculated source values and screenshot estimates. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 92 | - **Identifiers:** AV-066--AV-077; TR measurement facts. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 93 | ### Stage 3: classify findings | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 94 | - **Definition:** The audit step in which observed issues are mapped to AV failure modes and confirmed facts are mapped to TR/REF statements. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 95 | - **Role/domain:** Workflow; error taxonomy. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 96 | - **Caution:** Do not overgeneralize image-specific findings to other graphics. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 97 | - **Identifiers:** AV-001--AV-100; TR image observations. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 98 | ## B. Indexing, destination values, and recurrence | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 99 | ### Fv | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 100 | - **Definition:** The repository's symbol for a Fibonacci process step. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 101 | - **Role/domain:** Indexing; notation. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 102 | - **Caution:** Fv is not itself the destination value; avoid step-value swaps. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 103 | - **Identifiers:** TR-001; AV-006. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 104 | ### Fv convention | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 105 | - **Definition:** The document-defined process: `Fv -1 -> 0`, `Fv 0 -> 1`, `Fv 1 -> 1`, then addition of the two preceding destinations. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 106 | - **Role/domain:** Indexing; recurrence. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 107 | - **Caution:** Do not silently mix this with conventional `F_0 = 0, F_1 = 1` notation. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 108 | - **Identifiers:** TR-003--TR-007; AV-001--AV-005, AV-013; REF-001--REF-030. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 109 | ### Process step | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 110 | - **Definition:** A position in the Fv process, such as Fv 12, which has an associated destination D_12. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 111 | - **Role/domain:** Indexing. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 112 | - **Caution:** Distinguish process step from destination value, conventional index, transition, and ratio label. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 113 | - **Identifiers:** TR-001, TR-015; AV-006, AV-007. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 114 | ### Destination | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 115 | - **Definition:** The value reached at a process step; written `D_v` for step Fv v. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 116 | - **Role/domain:** Indexing; recurrence. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 117 | - **Caution:** Destination values are not interchangeable with Fv labels. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 118 | - **Identifiers:** TR-002; AV-006, AV-007, AV-092. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 119 | ### D_v | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 120 | - **Definition:** The notation for the destination value associated with Fv v. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 121 | - **Role/domain:** Notation; recurrence; ratio. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 122 | - **Caution:** In the repository convention, `D_v = F_(v+1)` under standard `F_0=0, F_1=1` indexing. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 123 | - **Identifiers:** TR-002, TR-007. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 124 | ### Fv -1 | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 125 | - **Definition:** The initial zero step in the repository convention, with destination 0. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 126 | - **Role/domain:** Indexing; seed values. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 127 | - **Caution:** Omitting this step is Zero Omission if the stated convention includes it. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 128 | - **Identifiers:** TR-003, TR-016; REF-001; AV-002. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 129 | ### Fv 0 | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 130 | - **Definition:** The first one step, with destination 1. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 131 | - **Role/domain:** Indexing; seed values. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 132 | - **Caution:** Do not merge it with Fv 1; the two ones occupy separate steps. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 133 | - **Identifiers:** TR-004, TR-017; REF-002; AV-003. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 134 | ### Fv 1 | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 135 | - **Definition:** The second one step, with destination 1, and the first step with a valid forward ratio `R_1 = D_1/D_0 = 1/1`. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 136 | - **Role/domain:** Indexing; seed values; ratio. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 137 | - **Caution:** The ratio is valid because the prior positive destination is D_0 = 1, not D_-1 = 0. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 138 | - **Identifiers:** TR-005, TR-018, TR-046; REF-003; AV-014. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 139 | ### Destination 0 | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 140 | - **Definition:** The canonical destination at Fv -1. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 141 | - **Role/domain:** Indexing; sequence value. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 142 | - **Caution:** It cannot be used as a denominator for a standard reciprocal or forward ratio. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 143 | - **Identifiers:** TR-003, TR-016; REF-001; AV-014. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 144 | ### Destination 1 | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 145 | - **Definition:** The destination at both Fv 0 and Fv 1. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 146 | - **Role/domain:** Indexing; seed values. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 147 | - **Caution:** The duplicate one is intentional and must not be collapsed into one step. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 148 | - **Identifiers:** TR-004, TR-005, TR-011, TR-017, TR-018; REF-002, REF-003; AV-003. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 149 | ### Seed destinations | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 150 | - **Definition:** The initial destination values that determine the recurrence, here 0, 1, and 1 as positioned by the Fv convention. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 151 | - **Role/domain:** Recurrence; indexing. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 152 | - **Caution:** A recurrence without seeds is underdetermined; wrong seed pairs create a different sequence. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 153 | - **Identifiers:** TR-003--TR-006; AV-005, AV-016. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 154 | ### Continuing by addition | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 155 | - **Definition:** The rule that every later destination is the sum of the two immediately preceding destinations. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 156 | - **Role/domain:** Recurrence. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 157 | - **Caution:** Addition must preserve process order and exact integer values. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 158 | - **Identifiers:** TR-006; AV-017, AV-020, AV-021, AV-026. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 159 | ### Recurrence | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 160 | - **Definition:** For `v >= 1`, the destination relation `D_v = D_(v-1) + D_(v-2)`. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 161 | - **Role/domain:** Recurrence; mathematical fact. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 162 | - **Caution:** Do not explain ratio convergence without also respecting the ratio recurrence where relevant. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 163 | - **Identifiers:** TR-006; AV-005, AV-016, AV-017, AV-040. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 164 | ### Conventional Fibonacci indexing | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 165 | - **Definition:** The external standard notation beginning `F_0 = 0` and `F_1 = 1`. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 166 | - **Role/domain:** Indexing; external mathematical context. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 167 | - **Caution:** In this repository, convert by `D_v = F_(v+1)` and never mix labels silently. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 168 | - **Identifiers:** TR-007; AV-004, AV-013. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 169 | ### Fv-to-conventional conversion | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 170 | - **Definition:** The mapping from repository steps to conventional Fibonacci labels: Fv v corresponds to conventional `F_(v+1)`. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 171 | - **Role/domain:** Indexing; notation. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 172 | - **Caution:** A chart using both systems must state the relationship explicitly. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 173 | - **Identifiers:** TR-007; AV-004, AV-013. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 174 | ### Conventional Map | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 175 | - **Definition:** The Truth Inventory's statement that `D_v = F_(v+1)` under conventional `F_0=0, F_1=1` indexing. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 176 | - **Role/domain:** Indexing. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 177 | - **Caution:** It is a conversion, not permission to relabel steps inconsistently. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 178 | - **Identifiers:** TR-007; AV-004, AV-013. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 179 | ### Canonical destination sequence | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 180 | - **Definition:** The inventory sequence from Fv -1 through Fv 28: 0, 1, 1, 2, 3, 5, 8, 13, ..., 514229. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 181 | - **Role/domain:** Recurrence; canonical reference. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 182 | - **Caution:** Values beyond the declared range may be Fibonacci values, but REF coverage ends at Fv 28. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 183 | - **Identifiers:** TR-016--TR-045; REF-001--REF-030. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 184 | ### Compact destination table | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 185 | - **Definition:** The Truth Inventory table mapping Fv steps -1 through 28 to destinations and conventional indices. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 186 | - **Role/domain:** Document structure; canonical reference. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 187 | - **Caution:** Use it to prevent copied-value and index errors. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 188 | - **Identifiers:** TR-016--TR-045; REF-001--REF-030; AV-094. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 189 | ### Thirty Values | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 190 | - **Definition:** The fact that Fv -1 through Fv 28 contains 30 destination values. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 191 | - **Role/domain:** Counting; indexing. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 192 | - **Caution:** Do not call these 30 values 30 transitions. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 193 | - **Identifiers:** TR-008; AV-008. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 194 | ### Twenty-Nine Transitions | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 195 | - **Definition:** The fact that the same Fv -1 through Fv 28 range contains 29 adjacent transitions. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 196 | - **Role/domain:** Counting; indexing. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 197 | - **Caution:** Transitions are between destinations, not destinations themselves. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 198 | - **Identifiers:** TR-009; AV-008. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 199 | ### Nonnegative destinations | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 200 | - **Definition:** Every canonical destination in the stated range is a nonnegative integer. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 201 | - **Role/domain:** Sequence value. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 202 | - **Caution:** Large unused negative plot ranges need a stated purpose. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 203 | - **Identifiers:** TR-010; AV-063. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 204 | ### Duplicate One / Twin One | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 205 | - **Definition:** The intentionally repeated positive destination 1 at Fv 0 and Fv 1. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 206 | - **Role/domain:** Indexing; seed values. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 207 | - **Caution:** Collapsing the two ones causes Twin-One Confusion. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 208 | - **Identifiers:** TR-011; AV-003. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 209 | ### Strict Growth | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 210 | - **Definition:** Destinations increase strictly from Fv 1 onward. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 211 | - **Role/domain:** Sequence property. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 212 | - **Caution:** Strict growth does not apply across Fv 0 to Fv 1 because both destinations are 1. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 213 | - **Identifiers:** TR-012. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 214 | ### Prior Value | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 215 | - **Definition:** The prior destination for Fv v is `D_(v-1)`. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 216 | - **Role/domain:** Indexing; ratio. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 217 | - **Caution:** A ratio annotation should not omit the prior destination used as denominator. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 218 | - **Identifiers:** TR-013; AV-009, AV-093. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 219 | ### Next Value | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 220 | - **Definition:** The destination after Fv v is `D_(v+1)`. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 221 | - **Role/domain:** Indexing; recurrence. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 222 | - **Caution:** Keep next-value language separate from Tomorrow in the metaphor. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 223 | - **Identifiers:** TR-014; AV-034. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 224 | ### Step Format | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 225 | - **Definition:** The unambiguous text form `Fv v -> destination D_v`. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 226 | - **Role/domain:** Notation; explanation. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 227 | - **Caution:** Use this format when labels might otherwise be mistaken for values. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 228 | - **Identifiers:** TR-015; AV-006, AV-007. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 229 | ### Index Drift | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 230 | - **Definition:** Shifting the same destination value among incompatible step numbers without declaring an indexing change. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 231 | - **Role/domain:** Indexing error. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 232 | - **Caution:** Especially likely when converting between Fv and conventional `F_n` notation. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 233 | - **Identifiers:** AV-001; TR-007. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 234 | ### Zero Omission | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 235 | - **Definition:** Beginning the displayed process at 1 while the stated convention includes `Fv -1 -> 0`. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 236 | - **Role/domain:** Indexing error. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 237 | - **Caution:** Omitting zero changes counts, transitions, and ratio-domain explanations. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 238 | - **Identifiers:** AV-002; TR-003, TR-016; REF-001. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 239 | ### Twin-One Confusion | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 240 | - **Definition:** Treating the two initial 1 destinations as one step. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 241 | - **Role/domain:** Indexing error. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 242 | - **Caution:** Fv 0 and Fv 1 must remain distinct. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 243 | - **Identifiers:** AV-003; TR-004, TR-005, TR-011. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 244 | ### Convention Mixing | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 245 | - **Definition:** Combining conventional `F_0=0` indexing with the Fv convention in one chart, caption, table, or equation without conversion. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 246 | - **Role/domain:** Indexing error; notation. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 247 | - **Caution:** State `D_v = F_(v+1)` whenever both systems appear. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 248 | - **Identifiers:** AV-004; TR-007. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 249 | ### Implicit Seeds | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 250 | - **Definition:** Presenting a recurrence without the seed destinations that determine it. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 251 | - **Role/domain:** Recurrence error. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 252 | - **Caution:** Different seed pairs can satisfy the same addition form but produce different sequences. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 253 | - **Identifiers:** AV-005; TR-003--TR-006. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 254 | ### Step-Value Swap | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 255 | - **Definition:** Using Fv as if it were both a step label and destination number. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 256 | - **Role/domain:** Terminology error. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 257 | - **Caution:** Separate Fv v from `D_v` with notation or prose. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 258 | - **Identifiers:** AV-006; TR-001, TR-002. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 259 | ### Term Ambiguity | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 260 | - **Definition:** Using term, step, index, value, and destination interchangeably. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 261 | - **Role/domain:** Terminology error. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 262 | - **Caution:** These words have distinct audit roles in the document set. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 263 | - **Identifiers:** AV-007; TR-001--TR-015. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 264 | ### Count Ambiguity | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 265 | - **Definition:** Confusing displayed destinations with adjacent transitions. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 266 | - **Role/domain:** Counting error. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 267 | - **Caution:** Fv -1 through Fv 28 has 30 destinations but 29 transitions. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 268 | - **Identifiers:** AV-008; TR-008, TR-009. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 269 | ### Missing Range / Endpoint Loss | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 270 | - **Definition:** Stopping before the declared endpoint or omitting final required destinations from a complete reference graphic. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 271 | - **Role/domain:** Range error; visualization. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 272 | - **Caution:** A complete 30-destination reference must include through Fv 28; endpoint loss specifically warns about Fv 23 through Fv 28. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 273 | - **Identifiers:** AV-010, AV-027; TR-040--TR-045; REF-025--REF-030. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 274 | ### Tick Gaps | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 275 | - **Definition:** Missing a step label on a sequential axis, such as skipping 22. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 276 | - **Role/domain:** Visualization; indexing error. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 277 | - **Caution:** A missing tick can falsely imply missing or shifted data. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 278 | - **Identifiers:** AV-011; TR image observations for Image Seven. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 279 | ### Duplicate Labels | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 280 | - **Definition:** Assigning one Fv label to two destinations or repeating a step label on an axis. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 281 | - **Role/domain:** Labeling error. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 282 | - **Caution:** Duplicate labels obscure the process-to-destination mapping. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 283 | - **Identifiers:** AV-012; TR-015. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 284 | ### Legacy Symbols | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 285 | - **Definition:** Retained `F_n` notation after relabeling data as Fv without stating the relationship. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 286 | - **Role/domain:** Notation error. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 287 | - **Caution:** Legacy symbols require explicit conversion to avoid convention mixing. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 288 | - **Identifiers:** AV-013; TR-007. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 289 | ## C. Ratios, limits, convergence, and the time metaphor | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 290 | ### Forward ratio | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 291 | - **Definition:** `R_v = D_v / D_(v-1)` for steps with a valid prior positive destination; it approaches phi. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 292 | - **Role/domain:** Ratio; convergence. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 293 | - **Caution:** It is not the reciprocal ratio and no finite forward ratio equals phi exactly. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 294 | - **Identifiers:** TR-046--TR-073; AV-014, AV-028, AV-031. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 295 | ### R_v | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 296 | - **Definition:** The Truth Inventory notation for the forward adjacent-destination ratio at Fv v. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 297 | - **Role/domain:** Ratio; notation. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 298 | - **Caution:** Its step label must correspond correctly to numerator and denominator. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 299 | - **Identifiers:** TR-046--TR-073; AV-009, AV-091. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 300 | ### Undefined Ratio | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 301 | - **Definition:** The error of assigning a forward ratio where no valid prior positive destination exists, notably Fv -1 or Fv 0. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 302 | - **Role/domain:** Ratio-domain error. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 303 | - **Caution:** Avoid zero denominators and absent prior positive destinations. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 304 | - **Identifiers:** AV-014; TR-046. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 305 | ### Fraction Offset | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 306 | - **Definition:** Labeling `D_v/D_(v-1)` with the wrong step, numerator, or denominator association. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 307 | - **Role/domain:** Ratio labeling error. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 308 | - **Caution:** State numerator and denominator definitions near ratio labels. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 309 | - **Identifiers:** AV-009; AV-091, AV-093. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 310 | ### Reciprocal ratio | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 311 | - **Definition:** `Q_v = D_(v-1) / D_v`, the reciprocal of the forward ratio where defined; it approaches `1/phi`. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 312 | - **Role/domain:** Ratio; convergence. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 313 | - **Caution:** Do not reverse it with `R_v`; no finite reciprocal ratio equals `1/phi` exactly. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 314 | - **Identifiers:** Reciprocal-ratio sample TR section; AV-028, AV-032. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 315 | ### Q_v | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 316 | - **Definition:** The Truth Inventory notation for reciprocal adjacent-destination ratios, sampled from Fv 1 through Fv 12. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 317 | - **Role/domain:** Ratio; notation. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 318 | - **Caution:** The reciprocal inventory is incomplete by design compared with the forward-ratio inventory through Fv 28. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 319 | - **Identifiers:** Reciprocal-ratio sample TR entries; AV-028, AV-030, AV-032. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 320 | ### R_1 = 1/1 | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 321 | - **Definition:** The first forward ratio, `D_1/D_0 = 1/1 = 1.000000000000`. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 322 | - **Role/domain:** Ratio; canonical value. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 323 | - **Caution:** It begins at Fv 1, not Fv -1 or Fv 0. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 324 | - **Identifiers:** TR-046; AV-014. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 325 | ### R_2 = 2/1 | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 326 | - **Definition:** The second forward ratio, `D_2/D_1 = 2/1 = 2.000000000000`. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 327 | - **Role/domain:** Ratio; canonical value. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 328 | - **Caution:** Its high value is part of the oscillatory convergence pattern. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 329 | - **Identifiers:** TR-047; AV-035, AV-036. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 330 | ### R_3 = 3/2 | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 331 | - **Definition:** The third forward ratio, `D_3/D_2 = 3/2 = 1.500000000000`. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 332 | - **Role/domain:** Ratio; canonical value. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 333 | - **Caution:** Keep the exact fraction when exactness matters. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 334 | - **Identifiers:** TR-048; AV-015. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 335 | ### R_4 = 5/3 | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 336 | - **Definition:** The fourth forward ratio, `D_4/D_3 = 5/3 ≈ 1.666666666667`. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 337 | - **Role/domain:** Ratio; canonical value. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 338 | - **Caution:** Decimal form is rounded; do not write it as exact equality to the rounded decimal. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 339 | - **Identifiers:** TR-049; AV-015. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 340 | ### R_28 = 514229/317811 | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 341 | - **Definition:** The forward ratio at Fv 28, `D_28/D_27 = 514229/317811 ≈ 1.618033988754`. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 342 | - **Role/domain:** Ratio; canonical endpoint. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 343 | - **Caution:** Despite being close to phi, it remains a finite rational ratio, not phi. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 344 | - **Identifiers:** TR-073; AV-031, AV-045. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 345 | ### Q_1 = 1/1 | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 346 | - **Definition:** The first reciprocal ratio, `D_0/D_1 = 1/1`. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 347 | - **Role/domain:** Ratio; canonical sample. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 348 | - **Caution:** It is a reciprocal-ratio value, not evidence that reciprocal ratios equal `1/phi`. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 349 | - **Identifiers:** Reciprocal-ratio sample TR entries; AV-032. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 350 | ### Q_2 = 1/2 | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 351 | - **Definition:** The reciprocal ratio `D_1/D_2 = 1/2`. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 352 | - **Role/domain:** Ratio; canonical sample. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 353 | - **Caution:** Do not plot it on a forward-ratio curve. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 354 | - **Identifiers:** Reciprocal-ratio sample TR entries; AV-028. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 355 | ### Q_12 = 144/233 | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 356 | - **Definition:** The reciprocal-ratio sample value at Fv 12, `D_11/D_12 = 144/233 ≈ 0.618025751073`. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 357 | - **Role/domain:** Ratio; canonical sample. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 358 | - **Caution:** It approximates `1/phi` but is not exactly `1/phi`. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 359 | - **Identifiers:** Reciprocal-ratio sample TR entries; AV-032. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 360 | ### Golden ratio / phi | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 361 | - **Definition:** `phi = (1 + sqrt(5)) / 2`, the irrational limiting value of forward Fibonacci ratios. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 362 | - **Role/domain:** Limit; external mathematical constant established in inventory. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 363 | - **Caution:** No finite ratio of integer Fibonacci destinations equals phi exactly. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 364 | - **Identifiers:** Golden Ratio and Forward Limit TR entries; AV-031, AV-041, AV-044. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 365 | ### Reciprocal limit / 1/phi | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 366 | - **Definition:** `1/phi = phi - 1`, the irrational limiting value of reciprocal Fibonacci ratios. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 367 | - **Role/domain:** Limit; ratio. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 368 | - **Caution:** No finite reciprocal ratio equals `1/phi` exactly. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 369 | - **Identifiers:** Reciprocal Limit TR entry; AV-028, AV-029, AV-032. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 370 | ### Forward Limit | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 371 | - **Definition:** The statement that forward ratios `R_v` approach phi as v increases. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 372 | - **Role/domain:** Convergence. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 373 | - **Caution:** Approach is alternating, not monotone. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 374 | - **Identifiers:** Forward Limit TR entry; AV-035, AV-036. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 375 | ### Ratio Update | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 376 | - **Definition:** The recurrence `R_(v+1) = 1 + 1/R_v` for forward ratios. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 377 | - **Role/domain:** Ratio recurrence; convergence. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 378 | - **Caution:** Omitting it weakens or obscures convergence explanations. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 379 | - **Identifiers:** Ratio Update TR entry; AV-040. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 380 | ### Error Identity | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 381 | - **Definition:** The signed-error relation `R_(v+1) - phi = -(R_v - phi)/(phi * R_v)`. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 382 | - **Role/domain:** Convergence; error analysis. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 383 | - **Caution:** It describes signed errors; do not confuse with absolute errors or step-to-step swings. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 384 | - **Identifiers:** Error Identity TR entry; AV-037, AV-038. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 385 | ### Alternating Sign | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 386 | - **Definition:** Forward-ratio errors alternate above and below phi. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 387 | - **Role/domain:** Convergence. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 388 | - **Caution:** Do not claim one-sided or monotone convergence. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 389 | - **Identifiers:** Alternating Sign TR entry; AV-035, AV-036. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 390 | ### Shrinking Error | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 391 | - **Definition:** The magnitudes of forward-ratio errors decrease as ratios converge toward phi. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 392 | - **Role/domain:** Convergence; error analysis. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 393 | - **Caution:** Shrinking error is not the same as a fixed exact multiplier at every step. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 394 | - **Identifiers:** Shrinking Error TR entry; AV-039. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 395 | ### Asymptotic Factor | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 396 | - **Definition:** The ratio of successive forward-error magnitudes approaches `1/phi^2`. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 397 | - **Role/domain:** Convergence; error analysis. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 398 | - **Caution:** The factor approaches `1/phi^2`; it is not exactly that factor at every finite step. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 399 | - **Identifiers:** Asymptotic Factor TR entry; AV-039. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 400 | ### Finite Rational | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 401 | - **Definition:** Every finite Fibonacci ratio formed from integer destinations is rational. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 402 | - **Role/domain:** Exactness; ratio. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 403 | - **Caution:** Finite rational ratios can approximate irrational limits but cannot equal them. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 404 | - **Identifiers:** Finite Rational TR entry; AV-031, AV-032. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 405 | ### Irrational Limit | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 406 | - **Definition:** Phi and `1/phi` are irrational limiting constants. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 407 | - **Role/domain:** Exactness; convergence. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 408 | - **Caution:** Decimal approximations are not exact symbolic values. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 409 | - **Identifiers:** Irrational Limit TR entry; AV-015, AV-031, AV-032. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 410 | ### No Equality | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 411 | - **Definition:** The inventory fact that no finite forward ratio equals phi exactly and no finite reciprocal ratio equals `1/phi` exactly. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 412 | - **Role/domain:** Exactness; ratio. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 413 | - **Caution:** Use `≈` for rounded numerical approximations. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 414 | - **Identifiers:** No Equality TR entry; AV-015, AV-031, AV-032. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 415 | ### Signed Error | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 416 | - **Definition:** A signed difference such as `R_v - phi`, retaining whether the ratio is above or below phi. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 417 | - **Role/domain:** Error analysis. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 418 | - **Caution:** Do not label it as absolute error. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 419 | - **Identifiers:** Signed Error TR entry; AV-038. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 420 | ### Absolute Error | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 421 | - **Definition:** A nonnegative distance such as `\|R_v - phi\|`. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 422 | - **Role/domain:** Error analysis. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 423 | - **Caution:** Do not confuse it with signed error or step-to-step ratio swing. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 424 | - **Identifiers:** Absolute Error TR entry; AV-037, AV-038. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 425 | ### Step Swing | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 426 | - **Definition:** The change between consecutive ratios, such as `\|R_v - R_(v-1)\|`. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 427 | - **Role/domain:** Error analysis; visualization. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 428 | - **Caution:** It is not the same quantity as distance from phi. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 429 | - **Identifiers:** Step Swing TR entry; AV-037. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 430 | ### Ratio Reversal | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 431 | - **Definition:** Confusing `D_v/D_(v-1)` with `D_(v-1)/D_v`. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 432 | - **Role/domain:** Ratio error. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 433 | - **Caution:** Forward ratios approach phi; reciprocal ratios approach `1/phi`. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 434 | - **Identifiers:** AV-028. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 435 | ### Exact Phi | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 436 | - **Definition:** The error of claiming a finite Fibonacci ratio exactly equals phi. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 437 | - **Role/domain:** Exactness error. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 438 | - **Caution:** Finite ratios are rational; phi is irrational. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 439 | - **Identifiers:** AV-031; Finite Rational, Irrational Limit, No Equality TR entries. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 440 | ### Exact Yesterday | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 441 | - **Definition:** The error of claiming a finite reciprocal ratio exactly equals `1/phi`. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 442 | - **Role/domain:** Exactness error; metaphor. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 443 | - **Caution:** `1/phi` is the reciprocal limit, not a finite reciprocal ratio. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 444 | - **Identifiers:** AV-032; Reciprocal Limit and No Equality TR entries. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 445 | ### Unmarked Approximation | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 446 | - **Definition:** Writing rounded decimals such as 0.618 or 1.618 with an equality sign. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 447 | - **Role/domain:** Exactness; notation error. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 448 | - **Caution:** Mark rounded decimals with `≈` or explicit wording. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 449 | - **Identifiers:** AV-015; Approximation Sign TR entry. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 450 | ### Decimal Truncation | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 451 | - **Definition:** Using too few decimals for phi when a chart claims to resolve late oscillations. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 452 | - **Role/domain:** Exactness; visualization. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 453 | - **Caution:** Insufficient precision can hide or fabricate above/below relationships. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 454 | - **Identifiers:** AV-044; AV-045. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 455 | ### Rounding Sign | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 456 | - **Definition:** Rounding late ratios so aggressively that above-phi and below-phi values appear identical. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 457 | - **Role/domain:** Exactness; rendering. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 458 | - **Caution:** Preserve enough precision or use exact fractions/error panels when sign matters. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 459 | - **Identifiers:** AV-045; Rounding Loss TR entry. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 460 | ### Yesterday, Today, Tomorrow metaphor | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 461 | - **Definition:** A document-defined metaphor mapping Yesterday to `1/phi ≈ 0.618`, Today to `1`, and Tomorrow to `phi ≈ 1.618`. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 462 | - **Role/domain:** Metaphor; visualization. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 463 | - **Caution:** It is not a Fibonacci theorem and does not redefine time or recurrence. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 464 | - **Identifiers:** Today Value, Yesterday Value, Tomorrow Value, Metaphor Status TR entries; AV-029--AV-034, AV-042. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 465 | ### Yesterday Value | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 466 | - **Definition:** The metaphorical reference value `1/phi = phi - 1 ≈ 0.618`. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 467 | - **Role/domain:** Metaphor; reciprocal limit. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 468 | - **Caution:** It belongs to the reciprocal-ratio limit, not the forward-ratio limit. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 469 | - **Identifiers:** Yesterday Value TR entry; AV-029, AV-032, AV-052. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 470 | ### Today Value / Unity Point | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 471 | - **Definition:** The metaphorical reference value `1`. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 472 | - **Role/domain:** Metaphor; reference line. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 473 | - **Caution:** Include it when the time metaphor is part of the display. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 474 | - **Identifiers:** Today Value and Unity Point TR entries; AV-042. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 475 | ### Tomorrow Value | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 476 | - **Definition:** The metaphorical reference value `phi ≈ 1.618`. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 477 | - **Role/domain:** Metaphor; forward limit. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 478 | - **Caution:** It belongs to the forward-ratio limit, not the reciprocal-ratio curve. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 479 | - **Identifiers:** Tomorrow Value TR entry; AV-030, AV-031. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 480 | ### Unequal Spacing | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 481 | - **Definition:** The fact that `1/phi`, `1`, and `phi` are not equally spaced on a linear number axis. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 482 | - **Role/domain:** Metaphor; visualization. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 483 | - **Caution:** Do not draw or imply equal spacing among Yesterday, Today, and Tomorrow on a linear scale. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 484 | - **Identifiers:** Unequal Spacing TR entry; AV-033. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 485 | ### Linear Time | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 486 | - **Definition:** The error of implying `0.618`, `1`, and `1.618` are equally spaced on a linear axis. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 487 | - **Role/domain:** Metaphor error; visualization. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 488 | - **Caution:** The labels are metaphorical references, not equal time intervals. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 489 | - **Identifiers:** AV-033; Unequal Spacing TR entry. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 490 | ### Metaphor Fact | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 491 | - **Definition:** The error of presenting Yesterday/Today/Tomorrow as a theorem of Fibonacci mathematics. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 492 | - **Role/domain:** Explanation error. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 493 | - **Caution:** Label the mapping as document-declared metaphor. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 494 | - **Identifiers:** AV-034; Metaphor Status TR entry. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 495 | ## D. Exactness, evidence, and mathematical context | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 496 | ### Exact fraction | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 497 | - **Definition:** A ratio represented symbolically as an integer numerator over an integer denominator, such as `233/144`. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 498 | - **Role/domain:** Exactness; ratio. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 499 | - **Caution:** Prefer exact fractions where equality matters; decimal expansions may be rounded. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 500 | - **Identifiers:** Forward-ratio TR entries; AV-015, AV-064. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 501 | ### Twelve-place decimal | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 502 | - **Definition:** The displayed decimal precision used in the forward-ratio inventory. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 503 | - **Role/domain:** Exactness; table representation. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 504 | - **Caution:** These decimals are rounded representations of exact fractions, not replacement exact values. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 505 | - **Identifiers:** TR-046--TR-073; AV-015, AV-064. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 506 | ### Approximation sign | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 507 | - **Definition:** The notation or wording indicating a rounded value, commonly `≈`. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 508 | - **Role/domain:** Exactness; notation. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 509 | - **Caution:** Use it for rounded phi, reciprocal phi, and finite ratio decimals. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 510 | - **Identifiers:** Approximation Sign TR entry; AV-015. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 511 | ### Mathematical exactness | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 512 | - **Definition:** Faithfulness to exact values, fractions, symbolic constants, and logical distinctions. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 513 | - **Role/domain:** Exactness; audit. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 514 | - **Caution:** Exactness can be lost through rounding, plotting resolution, screenshots, or verbal overclaiming. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 515 | - **Identifiers:** AV-015, AV-031, AV-032, AV-064, AV-098. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 516 | ### Rational approximation | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 517 | - **Definition:** A finite rational Fibonacci ratio used as an approximation to phi or `1/phi`. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 518 | - **Role/domain:** Ratio; convergence; external context. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 519 | - **Caution:** Approximation does not imply equality. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 520 | - **Identifiers:** Finite Rational, Irrational Limit, No Equality TR entries; AV-031, AV-032. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 521 | ### Convergence theorem versus inventory assertion (Supplemental) | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 522 | - **Definition:** The distinction between a fully proved mathematical theorem and the inventory's declarative statement of convergence facts. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 523 | - **Role/domain:** External mathematical context; document scope. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 524 | - **Caution:** The inventories state accepted facts for audit; they are not organized as a proof textbook. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 525 | - **Identifiers:** Forward Limit, Reciprocal Limit, Error Identity TR entries. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 526 | ### Data lineage | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 527 | - **Definition:** The trace from source Fibonacci values through calculations to displayed chart elements, labels, and prose. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 528 | - **Role/domain:** Workflow; audit evidence. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 529 | - **Caution:** Broken lineage permits copied errors, silent corrections, or source mismatch. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 530 | - **Identifiers:** AV-020--AV-025, AV-065, AV-094, AV-096. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 531 | ### Source-data-first principle | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 532 | - **Definition:** The rule that calculated source values are more authoritative than screenshot measurements when originals are available. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 533 | - **Role/domain:** Measurement; rendering; audit. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 534 | - **Caution:** Screenshots can be distorted by pixels, antialiasing, scaling, and export. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 535 | - **Identifiers:** AV-070, AV-077; Source Values TR entry. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 536 | ### Audit evidence classification | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 537 | - **Definition:** Separating what is mathematically verified, directly visible, screenshot-estimated, or indeterminate. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 538 | - **Role/domain:** Image audit; workflow. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 539 | - **Caution:** Do not promote an estimate to a verified fact. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 540 | - **Identifiers:** AV-067--AV-077; TR image-observation standards. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 541 | ### Directly visible evidence | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 542 | - **Definition:** Features that can be seen in an image without reconstructing missing data, such as labels, cropped elements, markers, or UI chrome. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 543 | - **Role/domain:** Image audit. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 544 | - **Caution:** Visible appearance may still be mathematically misleading. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 545 | - **Identifiers:** AV-074, AV-075; UI Element and Crop Fact TR entries. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 546 | ### Mathematically verified evidence | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 547 | - **Definition:** A finding confirmed by source values, formulas, recurrence checks, or exact construction rules. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 548 | - **Role/domain:** Audit; mathematics. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 549 | - **Caution:** Mathematical verification outranks visual resemblance. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 550 | - **Identifiers:** TR-006, TR-016--TR-073; AV-070, AV-098. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 551 | ### Screenshot-estimated evidence | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 552 | - **Definition:** A finding inferred from raster position, pixel measurement, or visible screenshot geometry. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 553 | - **Role/domain:** Image audit; rendering. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 554 | - **Caution:** Treat as limited by resolution, antialiasing, line width, crop, and scale. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 555 | - **Identifiers:** AV-067--AV-070, AV-074--AV-077. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 556 | ### Indeterminate evidence | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 557 | - **Definition:** A condition that cannot be decided from the available document, crop, resolution, scale, or labels. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 558 | - **Role/domain:** Image audit; workflow. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 559 | - **Caution:** State indeterminacy instead of inventing or assuming a rule. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 560 | - **Identifiers:** AV-098; missing-information guidance in Boot-Up Primer. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 561 | ### Word equation rendering loss (Supplemental) | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 562 | - **Definition:** Loss or placeholder corruption that can occur when equations from Word documents are extracted as plain text. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |

| 565 | - **Identifiers:** Supplemental; related to document fidelity requirements. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 566 | ### OCR-free text extraction (Supplemental) | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 567 | - **Definition:** Extracting text directly from document structure rather than recognizing rendered images of text. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 568 | - **Role/domain:** Document provenance. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 569 | - **Caution:** It avoids OCR errors but may still serialize tables or equations imperfectly. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |

| 576 | ## E. Chart construction and data visualization | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 577 | ### Discrete Data | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 578 | - **Definition:** Fibonacci destinations and ratios exist at integer process steps in this document set. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 579 | - **Role/domain:** Visualization; recurrence. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 580 | - **Caution:** Do not present them as continuous signals without markers at observations. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 581 | - **Identifiers:** Discrete Data TR entry; AV-046--AV-048. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 582 | ### Straight Segments | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 583 | - **Definition:** Line segments may connect discrete observations to guide the eye without inventing intermediate recurrence values. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 584 | - **Role/domain:** Visualization. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 585 | - **Caution:** The connecting line should not dominate the markers or imply a continuous process. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 586 | - **Identifiers:** Straight Segments TR entry; AV-047, AV-048, AV-062. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 587 | ### Spline Fiction | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 588 | - **Definition:** The error of using a smoothed spline through discrete Fibonacci ratios, thereby inventing intermediate values, crossings, and extrema. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 589 | - **Role/domain:** Visualization error. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 590 | - **Caution:** Use discrete markers and, if needed, straight connecting segments instead. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 591 | - **Identifiers:** AV-046; Spline Meaning TR entry. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 592 | ### Continuous Implication | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 593 | - **Definition:** Presenting integer-step recurrence data as if it were a continuous physical signal. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 594 | - **Role/domain:** Visualization error. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 595 | - **Caution:** Show markers for exact observations. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 596 | - **Identifiers:** AV-047; Discrete Data TR entry. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 597 | ### Marker Loss | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 598 | - **Definition:** A connected line without visible data markers when exact step positions matter. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 599 | - **Role/domain:** Visualization error. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 600 | - **Caution:** Fibonacci ratio and destination plots generally need markers to identify discrete steps. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 601 | - **Identifiers:** AV-048; Discrete Data TR entry. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 602 | ### Axis Identity | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 603 | - **Definition:** The requirement that each axis identify the quantity it represents, such as destination, forward ratio, reciprocal ratio, error, or Fv step. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 604 | - **Role/domain:** Visualization standard. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 605 | - **Caution:** Generic labels like “Value” or “Index” are insufficient when multiple quantities are possible. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |

| 607 | ### Vague Axis | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |

| 609 | - **Role/domain:** Visualization error. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |

| 611 | - **Identifiers:** AV-049. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 612 | ### Missing Units | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 613 | - **Definition:** An unlabeled dashed or guide line whose mathematical role is not defined. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
| 614 | - **Role/domain:** Visualization error. | Consistent with the shared corpus role and no contradiction identified. |
